## Analysis

The Ground Truth (GT) is:
$$-0.23236613283613416 \cdot A + 0.395876449251558 \cdot \sin(0.5265654762365851 \cdot A)$$

This has the form: `linear term in A` + `sin(linear term in A)`.

Let me check which candidates can match this form.

**Candidate 9: `A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2 + c3)`**

Setting:
- c0 = -0.23236613283613416
- c1 = 0.395876449251558
- c2 = 0.5265654762365851
- c3 = 0

This gives: `-0.23236613283613416*A + 0.395876449251558*sin(0.5265654762365851*A)`

This is exactly the GT. ✓

**Candidate 5: `A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2 + c3) + c4`** also works with c4=0.

**Candidate 8: `A*c0 + c1*cos(A*c2 + c3)`** works with c3 = π/2 since cos(x + π/2) = -sin(x), so c1 would be negated and c3 = π/2. Specifically: c0 = -0.232366..., c1 = -0.395876..., c2 = 0.526565..., c3 = π/2. This gives `A*c0 + c1*cos(A*c2 + π/2) = A*c0 - c1*sin(A*c2)` which matches. ✓

**Candidate 6: `A*c0 + c1 + c2*cos(A*c3 + c4)`** also works with c1=0 and appropriate phase shift.

Many other candidates also match by setting their extra parameters to zero, including candidates 4, 5, 6, 8, 9, 10, 11, 13, 14, 15, 16, 23, 25, 27, and many others.

The simplest and most direct match is **Candidate 9**.
